msg:I passed by Zibo this time and stayed for only one night. I chose the Sheraton Hotel. Because I am a Marriott Bonvoy member, the front desk upgraded the room for me. The wifi will automatically connect when you enter the room, which is very convenient. The room is clean and bright, with a good view. You can enjoy the beautiful sunset in the evening. The bedding and toiletries are of good quality, and it is very quiet to sleep at night. The breakfast is quite rich, the soy milk tastes very good, and I like to eat freshly made pancakes. Although I only stayed for one night, the hotel is very professional from the front desk, catering to room service, and it feels very comfortable. The only thing I have to complain about is the hotel parking lot. The sign is not too obvious. When leaving the garage, I turned around several times before I found the exit. Is this a way for the hotel to retain guests? Haha~

Location: It is next to the Mixc, and it takes about 10 minutes to walk to the Badaju. There are also mobile night market stalls at night. The recommended Sanwei Zhenhuo and Daxibei barbecued skewers are only about five minutes away on foot. Very convenient.

Service: The overall quality of the staff is good, and the service is meticulous and thoughtful. They will take the initiative to ask if there is anything they can help with. The room type was upgraded and the check-out time was delayed. The breakfast is also very good. You can't eat skewers every day. It is also very pleasant to enjoy the scenery on the 35th floor and the food in the bright restaurant on the second floor.

Worth recommending!

This has a lot to do with the location of the hotel

Lack of a heated swimming pool

msg:Went to Jinzi to catch a roast. After reading the reviews, this Sheraton was good and decisively booked. We drove there. The parking space was not good and the parking space was tight. We parked in the underground garage. The underground is shared with the shopping mall next to it. Check-in went smoothly. The young lady at the front desk was very nice. She gave the child breakfast and fruit as a gift, and added WeChat so that I could contact her anytime I needed anything. The room is on the 32nd floor. After entering, it does not match the photos on the reservation interface. The windows are not on the whole side, and there is a little wall in the middle. In the evening, the sudden heavy rain blew the window open, and it kept banging. The child was frightened by lightning and thunder. No one came to close the window after calling room service twice. The father of the child tried to close it by himself but couldn't close it. The lady at the front desk quickly had the staff close the window. Thanks again to the beautiful lady at the front desk. It rained suddenly again in the middle of the night. This time the window was not blown open. I heard the sound of rushing water. The child was so scared that he kept hugging me. At that time, the black light continued to put the child to sleep. When I woke up in the morning, I found that there was a water leak. My God, Is the five-star hotel good? One window has been tossing all night, and the child has been afraid. The window on the 32nd floor is not tight, and it leaks. How did your hotel do it? Besides, breakfast, from the time I went to eat to the time I finished eating, the sesame in the salad area The bowl of baking sauce is always empty, what does it mean? Can't afford it? If there is no stock, you can take it away. I went to it several times and the bowl was just quietly and empty. Why do you cut the waffles so small? You can cut a whole waffle into about ten small pieces for a poor little triangle. The child went to get a banana, which was astringent and raw, and took a bite. I just vomited. The best thing about the whole stay was the young lady at the front desk. I didn't remember her name. The other young lady who checked me out was also very good. Thank you very much. As for the other things, they really don't match the name of this hotel at all. It's too bad. The service of the restaurant can't keep up with it. They don't add things when they're gone. It's based on the principle of saving what you can.
The location of the hotel is very good, you can go to Badaju by walking, and the night view is also beautiful. It is very convenient to buy food and drink next to Vientiane.

posted:Posted May 19, 2023
msg:Great love for Zibo, the story of students repaying their kindness has been spread all over the country. We were deeply moved by traveling across peaks and traveling thousands of miles from Shenzhen to Zibo for roasting. I chose Sheraton Zibo Hotel, the No.1 luxury hotel, very comfortable and satisfied. The hotel's environmental facilities are modern and high-end, and the room interiors are upscale. The bedding is high quality and comfortable, and the walk-in cloakroom is great. The service is active, diligent and excellent. It was a pleasant surprise that the executive lounge changed the happy hour to the evening buffet. It shows the grand pattern and great wisdom. It is worth learning and promoting for Sheraton hotels all over the country. The breakfast and dinner buffets are very good, with a wide range of varieties, fast closing and good service. The evening buffet includes pancakes, scallions, skewers, dipping sauces, etc. The classic Yixiantian eating method is like a barbecue, which is hygienic, healthy and delicious. The hotel is located in the center of the city, very close to Badaju Food Street, less than 10 minutes walk, you can enjoy shopping and eating. Next door to the hotel is Vientiane Shopping Mall, which is very convenient for eating and shopping. I highly recommend the Sheraton Hotel when you come to Zibo!

posted:Posted May 23, 2023
msg:The hotel is located in the old town of Zhangdian, just a few steps from the road to Badaju. The hotel is directly connected to Vientiane Mall, the most powerful shopping mall in Zibo, which is very convenient.
On the first day of check-in, I encountered some facility problems, and the door of the room could not be hit. If you leave without checking after closing the door, you are still quite scared. It is recommended that everyone check in and confirm that the door is locked before leaving. The bathroom door was also derailed and took a lot of force to open. Fortunately, there were two people staying, and everyone worked hard to avoid being locked in the bathroom. The hotel quickly sent engineering personnel to check and arranged a new room in time, which is good.
The overall hardware facilities of the hotel are satisfactory, adding to the icing on the cake for the trip to Zibo. As one of the few international brand hotels in the city, it still makes people feel at ease during the journey.
